  <span m="737850">and</span> <span m="737950">also</span> <span m="738150">during</span>

  <span m="741080">us</span> <span m="741280">to do.</span></p><p><span m="744130">SABRINA
  DRAMMIS:</span> <span m="744610">So</span> <span m="744760">I''m</span> <span m="745140">going</span>

  <span m="759400">we</span> <span m="759500">thought</span> <span m="759690">it</span>
  <span m="759790">would</span> <span m="759890">be</span> <span m="759990">a</span>
  <span m="760090">great</span> <span m="760130">idea</span> <span m="760510">to use</span>
  <span m="760710">Phaser,</span> <span m="761310">which</span> <span m="761560">is</span>
  <span m="761700">a</span> <span m="761900">sprite-based</span> <span m="762980">game</span>
  <span m="763220">framework.</span></p><p><span m="764200">But</span> <span m="764590">as</span>

  <span m="1837110">it</span> <span m="1837760">was</span> <span m="1838130">time</span>

  <span m="1839240">every</span> <span m="1839470">second.</span> <span m="1839940">And</span>
  <span m="1840050">so</span> <span m="1840150">there</span> <span m="1840290">are</span>
  <span m="1840340">so</span> <span m="1840730">numbers</span> <span m="1841050">flying</span>
  <span m="1841320">at</span> <span m="1841450">people,</span> <span m="1841650">like</span>
  <span m="1841850">even</span> <span m="1842090">MIT</span> <span m="1842540">students</span>
  <span m="1842870">who</span> <span m="1842990">play</span> <span m="1843100">tested</span>
  <span m="1843410">it</span> <span m="1843500">couldn''t</span> <span m="1843680">understand.</span></p><p><span

  <span m="1845240">that</span> <span m="1845950">people</span> <span m="1846170">like</span>
  <span m="1846340">policymakers,</span> <span m="1846920">who</span> <span m="1846990">didn''t</span>
  <span m="1847180">have</span> <span m="1847320">much</span> <span m="1847470">experience</span>

  <span m="1849280">wouldn''t</span> <span m="1849500">be</span> <span m="1849580">able</span>

  <span m="5988240">For</span> <span m="5988370">example,</span> <span m="5988760">with</span>
  <span m="5988870">the</span> <span m="5988950">facility</span> <span m="5989430">game</span>
  <span m="5990480">at</span> <span m="5990680">the</span> <span m="5990740">beginning</span>
  <span m="5991080">when</span> <span m="5991200">we</span> <span m="5991270">had</span>
  <span m="5991610">the</span> <span m="5991860">very</span> <span m="5992090">fast-paced</span>
  <span m="5992610">clicking,</span> <span m="5993000">and</span> <span m="5993100">then</span>
  <span m="5993210">you</span> <span m="5993290">would</span> <span m="5993410">fail</span>
  <span m="5993940">almost all</span> <span m="5994140">the</span> <span m="5994220">time.</span>
  <span m="5994660">We</span> <span m="5994890">wanted</span> <span m="5995080">to</span>
  <span m="5995200">make</span> <span m="5995330">sure</span> <span m="5995480">that</span>
  <span m="5995630">it</span> <span m="5995700">wasn''t</span> <span m="5996010">too</span>
  <span m="5996150">difficult,</span> <span m="5997140">and</span> <span m="5997270">that</span>
  <span m="5997410">it</span> <span m="5997460">was</span> <span m="5997680">accessible.</span></p><p><span
  m="5999410">The</span> <span m="5999490">cultural</span> <span m="5999790">disconnect</span>
  <span m="6000200">we</span> <span m="6000500">touched</span> <span m="6000840">a</span>
  <span m="6000880">bit</span> <span m="6001040">on</span> <span m="6001430">in</span>
  <span m="6001760">some</span> <span m="6001910">of</span> <span m="6001970">our</span>
  <span m="6002100">previous</span> <span m="6002500">games,</span> <span m="6003260">making</span>
  <span m="6003570">sure</span> <span m="6003780">that</span> <span m="6004660">the</span>
  <span m="6005070">target</span> <span m="6005420">audience</span> <span m="6005850">will</span>
  <span m="6006000">be</span> <span m="6006130">able</span> <span m="6006300">to</span>
  <span m="6006440">play</span> <span m="6006640">this</span> <span m="6006820">game</span>
  <span m="6007010">and</span> <span m="6007090">relate</span> <span m="6007450">to</span>
  <span m="6007590">it</span> <span m="6007890">in</span> <span m="6008030">order</span>
  <span m="6008190">to</span> <span m="6008550">pull</span> <span m="6008710">the</span>
  <span m="6008780">message</span> <span m="6009140">from it,</span> <span m="6010050">and</span>
  <span m="6010300">making</span> <span m="6010550">the</span> <span m="6010630">play</span>
  <span m="6010840">meaningful.</span> <span m="6011500">We</span> <span m="6011710">wanted</span>
  <span m="6012040">to</span> <span m="6012170">make</span> <span m="6012360">sure</span>
  <span m="6012710">that</span> <span m="6013170">the</span> <span m="6013920">game</span>
  <span m="6014110">play</span> <span m="6014270">was</span> <span m="6014430">still</span>
  <span m="6014640">getting</span> <span m="6014830">the</span> <span m="6014900">message</span>
  <span m="6015210">across,</span> <span m="6015840">and</span> <span m="6016090">finding</span>
  <span m="6016400">a</span> <span m="6016450">good</span> <span m="6016640">balance</span>
  <span m="6016950">between</span> <span m="6017270">education</span> <span m="6017850">and</span>
  <span m="6018120">play.</span></p><p><span m="6020148">RACHEL WANG:</span> <span
  m="6020590">So</span> <span m="6020730">now</span> <span m="6020940">I''ll</span>
  <span m="6021030">talk</span> <span m="6021220">about</span> <span m="6021620">how</span>
  <span m="6021980">our</span> <span m="6022190">teamwork</span> <span m="6022620">worked
  out,</span> <span m="6023060">and</span> <span m="6023250">what</span> <span m="6023410">our</span>
  <span m="6023490">process</span> <span m="6024020">like</span> <span m="6024210">as</span>
  <span m="6024390">a</span> <span m="6024460">team.</span> <span m="6025130">So we</span>
  <span m="6025350">used</span> <span m="6025660">four</span> <span m="6025980">main</span>
  <span m="6026740">tools.</span> <span m="6027290">The</span> <span m="6027300">first</span>
  <span m="6027550">one</span> <span m="6027670">being</span> <span m="6027910">Trello,</span>
  <span m="6028710">to</span> <span m="6028840">keep</span> <span m="6029050">track</span>
  <span m="6029360">of</span> <span m="6029720">our</span> <span m="6029890">tasks</span>
  <span m="6030370">and</span> <span m="6030490">progresses.</span> <span m="6031100">So,</span>
  <span m="6031650">we''d</span> <span m="6031880">put</span> <span m="6032040">all</span>
  <span m="6032310">our</span> <span m="6032440">sprint</span> <span m="6032740">task</span>
  <span m="6033045">lists,</span> <span m="6033350">our</span> <span m="6033440">product</span>
  <span m="6033780">backlog,</span> <span m="6034270">on</span> <span m="6034470">to</span>
  <span m="6034590">the</span> <span m="6034710">Trello.</span> <span m="6035440">People
  would</span> <span m="6035770">claim</span> <span m="6036130">the</span> <span m="6036220">different</span>
  <span m="6036520">tasks,</span> <span m="6036900">and</span> <span m="6037070">then</span>
  <span m="6037590">be</span> <span m="6037690">able</span> <span m="6037800">to</span>
  <span m="6037920">say</span> <span m="6038150">if</span> <span m="6038270">they</span>
  <span m="6038380">were</span> <span m="6038500">doing</span> <span m="6038840">them,</span>
  <span m="6039050">if</span> <span m="6039160">they were</span> <span m="6039340">done,</span>
  <span m="6039660">or</span> <span m="6039750">if</span> <span m="6039840">they</span>
  <span m="6039930">haven''t</span> <span m="6040280">started.</span> <span m="6041340">And</span>
  <span m="6041530">then</span> <span m="6041680">that</span> <span m="6041890">means</span>
  <span m="6042150">we</span> <span m="6042260">could</span> <span m="6042700">track</span>
  <span m="6043050">how</span> <span m="6043220">people''s</span> <span m="6043570">progress</span>
  <span m="6044000">was.</span></p><p><span m="6045670">The</span> <span m="6045790">second</span>
  <span m="6046080">one</span> <span m="6046270">was</span> <span m="6046440">weekly</span>
  <span m="6046750">meetings.</span> <span m="6047200">So,</span> <span m="6047540">every
  week</span> <span m="6047790">we</span> <span m="6047890">had</span> <span m="6048030">a</span>
  <span m="6048080">meeting</span> <span m="6048510">to</span> <span m="6049120">either</span>

  <span m="6050100">about</span> <span m="6050260">Ghana,</span> <span m="6050770">talk</span>
  <span m="6051020">about</span> <span m="6051180">how</span> <span m="6051320">we</span>
  <span m="6051450">could</span> <span m="6051590">improve</span> <span m="6052710">the</span>
  <span m="6052840">game</span> <span m="6053090">play and</span> <span m="6053330">make</span>
  <span m="6053540">it</span> <span m="6053620">more</span> <span m="6053770">meaningful,</span>
  <span m="6054820">if</span> <span m="6054970">we</span> <span m="6055080">should</span>
  <span m="6055250">cut</span> <span m="6055470">some</span> <span m="6055660">features,</span>
  <span m="6056420">and</span> <span m="6056620">whatnot.</span> <span m="6057140">So,</span>
  <span m="6057530">these</span> <span m="6057720">meetings</span> <span m="6058080">were</span>
  <span m="6058170">really</span> <span m="6058360">great</span> <span m="6058710">for</span>
  <span m="6059090">quick</span> <span m="6059340">and</span> <span m="6059420">efficient</span>
  <span m="6060740">decisions,</span> <span m="6061380">and</span> <span m="6061600">also</span>
  <span m="6061920">really</span> <span m="6062160">important</span> <span m="6062520">decisions.</span></p><p><span
  m="6063590">Our</span> <span m="6063760">third</span> <span m="6064000">tool</span>
  <span m="6064200">was</span> <span m="6064370">Slack,</span> <span m="6064890">which</span>
  <span m="6065520">some</span> <span m="6065690">other</span> <span m="6065890">teams</span>
  <span m="6066130">talked</span> <span m="6066420">about.</span> <span m="6066755">But
  it</span> <span m="6067090">was</span> <span m="6067250">really</span> <span m="6067490">great</span>
  <span m="6067830">because,</span> <span m="6068390">first,</span> <span m="6068630">they</span>
  <span m="6068720">had</span> <span m="6069830">Google</span> <span m="6070130">Drive</span>
  <span m="6070470">integration,</span> <span m="6071080">so</span> <span m="6071230">you</span>
  <span m="6071430">could</span> <span m="6071600">see</span> <span m="6072210">when</span>
  <span m="6072450">people</span> <span m="6072690">were</span> <span m="6072850">pushing</span>
  <span m="6073230">code</span> <span m="6073590">if</span> <span m="6073690">you</span>
  <span m="6073800">should</span> <span m="6073990">be</span> <span m="6074130">pulling</span>
  <span m="6074490">code.</span> <span m="6075440">And</span> <span m="6075540">then,</span>
  <span m="6075710">in</span> <span m="6075820">addition,</span> <span m="6076310">we</span>
  <span m="6076410">could</span> <span m="6076510">have</span> <span m="6076560">different</span>
  <span m="6076890">channels.</span> <span m="6077750">So</span> <span m="6078060">we</span>
  <span m="6078180">had</span> <span m="6078320">a</span> <span m="6078550">separate</span>
  <span m="6079010">coding</span> <span m="6079730">channel,</span> <span m="6080170">where</span>
  <span m="6080390">all</span> <span m="6080520">the</span> <span m="6080610">coders</span>
  <span m="6082180">could</span> <span m="6082380">talk</span> <span m="6082680">to</span>
  <span m="6082790">each</span> <span m="6082980">other,</span> <span m="6083510">and</span>
  <span m="6083720">that</span> <span m="6083870">might</span> <span m="6084020">not</span>
  <span m="6084170">be</span> <span m="6084300">relevant</span> <span m="6084760">to</span>
  <span m="6084830">other</span> <span m="6085060">people.</span> <span m="6086000">And</span>
  <span m="6086070">then</span> <span m="6086210">having</span> <span m="6086540">a</span>
  <span m="6086580">whole</span> <span m="6086820">team</span> <span m="6087670">channel</span>
  <span m="6088050">was also</span> <span m="6088370">efficient,</span> <span m="6088800">because</span>
  <span m="6089180">it</span> <span m="6089300">would</span> <span m="6089460">be</span>
  <span m="6089630">faster</span> <span m="6090090">response</span> <span m="6090620">than</span>
  <span m="6090800">email.</span></p><p><span m="6092500">And</span> <span m="6092620">then</span>
  <span m="6092800">our</span> <span m="6092870">final one</span> <span m="6093260">was</span>
  <span m="6093450">Google</span> <span m="6093720">Drive,</span> <span m="6094040">which</span>
  <span m="6094190">is</span> <span m="6094310">where</span> <span m="6094480">we</span>
  <span m="6094610">have</span> <span m="6095210">all</span> <span m="6095400">our</span>
  <span m="6095520">assets,</span> <span m="6096180">had all</span> <span m="6096510">our</span>
  <span m="6096800">dialogues,</span> <span m="6097350">our</span> <span m="6097460">characters.</span>
  <span m="6098500">And</span> <span m="6098920">this</span> <span m="6099000">worked
  out</span> <span m="6099160">to be</span> <span m="6099400">a</span> <span m="6099500">really</span>
  <span m="6099750">great</span> <span m="6099990">tool</span> <span m="6100280">for</span>
  <span m="6101350">collaborative</span> <span m="6101930">storage.</span></p><p><span
  m="6103830">Some</span> <span m="6104030">downfalls</span> <span m="6104570">of</span>
  <span m="6104980">this</span> <span m="6105420">was--</span> <span m="6106390">I''ll</span>
  <span m="6106770">talk</span> <span m="6106930">about</span> <span m="6107140">the</span>
  <span m="6108150">second</span> <span m="6108470">part,</span> <span m="6108860">was</span>

  <span m="6111810">these</span> <span m="6112000">tools</span> <span m="6112320">you</span>

  <span m="6113960">tools.</span> <span m="6114390">It''s</span> <span m="6114710">not</span>
  <span m="6114860">actually</span> <span m="6115440">effective</span> <span m="6115910">to</span>

  <span m="6118870">found</span> <span m="6119100">this</span> <span m="6119260">to</span>

  <span m="6120640">updating</span> <span m="6121000">their</span> <span m="6121110">progress</span>

  <span m="6124880">mitigations</span> <span m="6125320">we</span> <span m="6125410">had</span>
  <span m="6125600">to</span> <span m="6125690">that</span> <span m="6125950">is,

  <span m="6126860">can</span> <span m="6127020">mention</span> <span m="6127450">people''s</span>
  <span m="6128150">names,</span> <span m="6128520">and</span> <span m="6128630">then</span>

  <span m="6141090">I</span> <span m="6141470">think</span> <span m="6141680">we</span>
  <span m="6141940">worked</span> <span m="6142220">it</span> <span m="6142300">out.</span></p><p><span

  <span m="6143740">have</span> <span m="6143860">improved</span> <span m="6144200">on</span>
  <span m="6144460">was</span> <span m="6144820">enforcing</span> <span m="6146020">deadlines,</span>

  <span m="6147900">As</span> <span m="6148120">Kevin</span> <span m="6148350">will</span>

  <span m="6154020">obviously</span> <span m="6154500">the</span> <span m="6154680">art</span>
  <span m="6154900">assets</span> <span m="6155240">had to be</span> <span m="6155370">done</span>

  <span m="6157620">and</span> <span m="6157860">put it</span> <span m="6158020">into</span>
  <span m="6158260">the</span> <span m="6158370">game.</span> <span m="6159000">So</span>
  <span m="6159400">in</span> <span m="6160640">that</span> <span m="6161050">aspect,</span>
  <span m="6161490">we</span> <span m="6161560">should</span> <span m="6161730">have</span>
  <span m="6161860">probably</span> <span m="6162170">had</span> <span m="6162500">clearer</span>
  <span m="6162790">deadlines</span> <span m="6163300">so</span> <span m="6163560">that</span>
  <span m="6164100">we</span> <span m="6164600">could</span> <span m="6164830">stick</span>

  <span m="6166670">schedule.</span> <span m="6167950">And</span> <span m="6168100">then,</span>
  <span m="6168770">in</span> <span m="6168870">addition,</span> <span m="6169290">we</span>
  <span m="6169870">should</span> <span m="6170080">have</span> <span m="6170260">probably</span>
  <span m="6170610">had</span> <span m="6170880">a</span> <span m="6170930">bit</span>
  <span m="6171140">more</span> <span m="6171850">frequent</span> <span m="6172280">communication</span>
  <span m="6173250">with the</span> <span m="6173460">entire</span> <span m="6173880">team.</span>
  <span m="6174520">So</span> <span m="6174700">we</span> <span m="6174790">did</span>
  <span m="6174960">have</span> <span m="6175140">a</span> <span m="6175200">lot</span>
  <span m="6175420">of</span> <span m="6175520">communication,</span> <span m="6176220">but</span>
  <span m="6176470">sometimes</span> <span m="6177320">not</span> <span m="6177470">all</span>

  <span m="6179650">we</span> <span m="6180360">should</span> <span m="6180570">have</span>
  <span m="6180730">probably</span> <span m="6181050">improved</span> <span m="6181390">a</span>
  <span m="6181450">bit</span> <span m="6181630">about</span> <span m="6181980">sending</span>
  <span m="6182800">out</span> <span m="6182950">meeting</span> <span m="6183240">notes</span>
  <span m="6183610">and</span> <span m="6183990">catching</span> <span m="6184360">up</span>
